TUR_minority_revolt_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_controlled_state = {
					TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = yes
					resistance > 74.9
				}
			}
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = yes
					resistance > 74.9
				}
				controller = { country_event = { id = ottoman.0 hours = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_reduce_armenian_christian_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { state = 352 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.101 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 806 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.103 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1022 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.134 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 881 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.135 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 355 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.136 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1025 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.135 days = 4 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_resistance = yes
				is_core_of = ROOT
				TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = no
			}
			cancel_resistance = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = ARM }
			remove_core_of = ARM
			if = {
				limit = { state = 353 }
				354 = { remove_claim_by = ARM }
				1034 = { remove_claim_by = ARM }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_reduce_armenian_population
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_armenian_minority
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_attrition_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_army_defence_factor_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_enemy_local_supplies_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_recruitable_population_armenian_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = -1 }
	add_to_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level = -20 }
	add_to_variable = { TUR_apostolic_state_level = -1 }
}

TUR_reduce_greek_christian_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek = -0.1 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek = -0.02 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek
			min = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_resistance = yes
				is_core_of = ROOT
				TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = no
			}
			cancel_resistance = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = GRE }
			remove_core_of = GRE
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = PON }
			remove_core_of = PON
			if = {
				limit = { state = 354 }
				1034 = { remove_claim_by = PON }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_reduce_greek_population
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_greek_minority
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_resources_factor_greek_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_intel_to_enemies_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek = -0.1 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_recruitable_population_greek_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_construction_speed_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek = -0.02 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level = -1 }
	add_to_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level = -20 }
	add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = -1 }
}

TUR_reduce_greek_muslim_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level < 2 } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek = 0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek
				max = 0
			}
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek = -0.1 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek
				min = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = TUR_greek_sunni_state_level
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level = 0 } }
				}
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_greek = 0.05 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek = -0.02 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek
				min = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_resistance = yes
					is_core_of = ROOT
					TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = no
				}
				cancel_resistance = yes
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_reduce_greek_population
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_greek_minority
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_resources_factor_greek_down
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek = 0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_local_resources_factor_greek
				max = 0
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_intel_to_enemies_down
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek = -0.1 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_local_intel_to_enemies_greek
				min = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = TUR_greek_sunni_state_level
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level = 0 } }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_resistance_target_down
				add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_greek = 0.05 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_construction_speed_down
			add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_greek = -0.02 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek
				max = 0
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level = -1 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level = -20 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = -1 }
	}
}

		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { TUR_arab_shia_state_level = -20 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_shia_state_level = -1 }
		}
	}
}
TUR_reduce_arab_christian_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_supplies_for_controller_arab = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_supplies_for_controller_arab
			max = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_resistance = yes
				is_core_of = ROOT
				TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = no
			}
			cancel_resistance = yes
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_reduce_arab_population
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_arab_minority
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_local_supplies_for_controller_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_local_supplies_for_controller_arab = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_local_supplies_for_controller_arab
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level = -1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_variable = TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level }
						check_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level = 0 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level = -20 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = -1 }
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_variable = TUR_arab_catholic_state_level }
						check_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level = 0 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level = -20 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_catholic_state_level = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level = -1 }
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_variable = TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level }
						check_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level = 0 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level = -20 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = -1 }
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_variable = TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level }
						check_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level = 0 }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level = -20 }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_catholic_state_level = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_reduce_albanian_muslim_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_resistance_growth_albanian = -0.1 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_resistance_growth_albanian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_albanian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_albanian
			max = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_resistance = yes
				is_core_of = ROOT
				TUR_state_has_minority_modifier = no
			}
			cancel_resistance = yes
		}

	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_reduce_albanian_population
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_albanian_minority

TUR_increase_christian_conscriptions_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
			check_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_greek < 0 }

			tooltip = recruitable_population_factor_5

ottoman_minority_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		ottoman_start_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_armenian_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_greek_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_arab_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_jewish_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_south_slavic_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_albanian_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_kurdish_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_assyrian_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_georgian_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_turkish_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_all_variable_check = yes
	}
}

ottoman_armenian_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_variable = ROOT.TUR_armenian_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_variable = ROOT.TUR_apostolic_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_variable = TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_variable = TUR_armenian_apostolic_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_temp_variable = 0 } } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_variable = TUR_armenian_temp_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_variable = TUR_armenian_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = TUR_armenian_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_armenian_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		}
		341 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_341_armenian_population_stability_factor = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor } }
		347 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_347_armenian_population_stability_factor = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor } }
		1019 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1019_armenian_population_stability_factor = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor } }
		1035 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1035_armenian_population_stability_factor = TUR_armenian_population_stability_factor } }

		ottoman_all_variable_check = yes
	}

ottoman_greek_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = ROOT.TUR_greek_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_variable = ROOT.TUR_sunni_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_variable = TUR_greek_sunni_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = TUR_greek_sunni_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_variable = ROOT.TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_variable = TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = TUR_greek_orthodox_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = TUR_greek_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = TUR_greek_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		}
		164 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_164_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		182 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_182_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		183 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_183_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		184 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_184_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		185 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_185_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		187 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_187_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		200 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_200_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		339 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_339_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		341 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_341_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		342 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_342_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		345 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_345_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }
		347 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_347_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor } }

ottoman_arab_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = ROOT.TUR_arab_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_variable = ROOT.TUR_sunni_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_variable = TUR_arab_sunni_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = TUR_arab_sunni_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_variable = ROOT.TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_variable = TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = TUR_arab_orthodox_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_shia_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_shia_variable = ROOT.TUR_shia_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_shia_variable = TUR_arab_shia_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_shia_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = TUR_arab_shia_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_variable = ROOT.TUR_catholic_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_variable = TUR_arab_catholic_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = TUR_arab_catholic_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_temp_variable = 0 } } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = TUR_arab_temp_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = TUR_arab_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = TUR_arab_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = TUR_arab_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_arab_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_arab_population_stability_factor

ottoman_arab_variable_check_only = {
	hidden_effect = {
		ottoman_start_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_arab_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_all_variable_check = yes
	}
}

ottoman_jewish_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_jewish_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = ROOT.TUR_jewish_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_variable = ROOT.TUR_judaic_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_variable = TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = TUR_jewish_judaic_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = TUR_jewish_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_jewish_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_jewish_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		}
		345 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_345_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor } }
		347 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_347_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor } }
		454 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_454_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor } }
		756 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_756_jewish_population_stability_factor = TUR_jewish_population_stability_factor } }
		345 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_345_jewish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor } }
		347 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_347_jewish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor } }
		454 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_454_jewish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor } }
		756 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_756_jewish_population_war_support_factor = TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor } }
	}
}
ottoman_jewish_variable_check_only = {
	hidden_effect = {
		ottoman_start_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_jewish_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_all_variable_check = yes
	}
}

ottoman_south_slavic_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = ROOT.TUR_south_slavic_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_variable = ROOT.TUR_sunni_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_variable = TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = TUR_south_slavic_sunni_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_variable = ROOT.TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_variable = TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_variable = ROOT.TUR_catholic_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_variable = TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = TUR_south_slavic_catholic_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_temp_variable = 0 } } }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = TUR_south_slavic_temp_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = TUR_south_slavic_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = TUR_south_slavic_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = TUR_south_slavic_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = 9 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = 9 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_south_slavic_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		}

ottoman_albanian_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_variable = ROOT.TUR_albanian_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_variable = ROOT.TUR_sunni_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_variable = TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_variable = TUR_albanian_sunni_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_variable = ROOT.TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_variable = TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_variable = TUR_albanian_orthodox_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_variable = ROOT.TUR_catholic_population_factor_variable }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_variable = TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_variable = TUR_albanian_catholic_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_variable = TUR_albanian_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = TUR_albanian_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_albanian_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_state_level > 0 } }
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		}

ottoman_assyrian_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_variable = ROOT.TUR_assyrian_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_syriac_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_syriac_variable = ROOT.TUR_shia_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_syriac_variable = TUR_assyrian_syriac_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_syriac_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_variable = TUR_assyrian_syriac_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_variable = TUR_assyrian_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_assyrian_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor = TUR_assyrian_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_assyrian_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}

		350 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_350_assyrian_population_stability_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor } }
		828 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_828_assyrian_population_stability_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor } }
		1028 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1028_assyrian_population_stability_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor } }
		884 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_884_assyrian_population_stability_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor } }
		879 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_879_assyrian_population_stability_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_stability_factor } }
		350 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_350_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor } }
		828 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_828_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor } }
		1028 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1028_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor } }
		884 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_884_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor } }
		879 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_879_assyrian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor } }
	}

ottoman_georgian_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_variable = ROOT.TUR_georgian_population_factor_variable }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_variable = ROOT.TUR_shia_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_variable = TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_variable = TUR_georgian_sunni_variable }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_variable = ROOT.TUR_shia_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_variable = TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_variable = TUR_georgian_orthodox_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_variable = TUR_georgian_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = TUR_georgian_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_georgian_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
			}
        	if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = 5 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ARM } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = 8 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = 8 }
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority } }
							NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_state_level > 0 } }
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
							}
							AND = {
								has_variable = TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor
								NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor = 0 }
		}
		816 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_816_georgian_population_stability_factor = TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor } }
		855 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_855_georgian_population_stability_factor = TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor } }
		1034 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1034_georgian_population_stability_factor = TUR_georgian_population_stability_factor } }
		816 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_816_georgian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor } }
		855 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_855_georgian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor } }
		1034 = { set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_1034_georgian_population_war_support_factor = TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor } }
	}
}

ottoman_turkish_variable_check_only = {
	hidden_effect = {
		ottoman_start_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_turkish_variable_check = yes
		ottoman_all_variable_check = yes
	}
}

ottoman_start_variable_check = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_factor_variable = TUR_armenian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_factor_variable = TUR_greek_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_factor_variable = TUR_jewish_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_factor_variable = TUR_arab_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_factor_variable = TUR_south_slavic_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_factor_variable = TUR_albanian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_factor_variable = TUR_kurdish_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_factor_variable = TUR_assyrian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_factor_variable = TUR_georgian_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_factor_variable = TUR_turkish_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable = TUR_orthodox_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_factor_variable = TUR_apostolic_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_judaic_population_factor_variable = TUR_judaic_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_factor_variable = TUR_syriac_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_factor_variable = TUR_catholic_population_factor }
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_adem_i_merkeziyetcilik }
			divide_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_factor_variable = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_autonomy_in_non_muslim_vilayets }
			set_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_factor_variable = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_judaic_population_factor_variable = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_factor_variable = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_factor_variable = 0 }
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_autonomy_lebanon_factor_tt = TUR_ottoman_autonomy_lebanon_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_autonomy_factor_tt = TUR_ottoman_autonomy_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_ottoman_semi_autonomy_factor_tt = TUR_ottoman_semi_autonomy_factor }
	}
}

		multiply_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_stability_half_positive = -1 }
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = 0 }
		every_state = {
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_minority_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_armenian_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_jewish_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_south_slavic_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_albanian_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_kurdish_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_assyrian_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_georgian_population_war_support_factor }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = THIS.TUR_turkish_population_war_support_factor }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_autonomy_lebanon_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_autonomy_lebanon_factor }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_autonomy_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_autonomy_factor }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_state_has_semi_autonomy_mtth = yes }
				add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_sublime_realm_war_support = ROOT.TUR_ottoman_semi_autonomy_factor }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_half = TUR_sublime_realm_war_support }
		divide_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_half = 2 }
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_positive = TUR_sublime_realm_war_support }
		multiply_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_positive = -1 }
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_half_positive = TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_half }
		multiply_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_war_support_half_positive = -1 }
		#mecca resistance value
		670 = { set_variable = { global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target = TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_arab } }
		add_to_variable = { global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target = -0.1 }
		set_variable = { global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target_opposite = global.TUR_mecca_resistance_target }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		set_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_tt = TUR_armenian_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_tt = TUR_greek_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_tt = TUR_jewish_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_arab_population_tt = TUR_arab_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_tt = TUR_south_slavic_population_factor_variable }

		set_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_tt = TUR_kurdish_population_factor_variable }

		set_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_tt = TUR_georgian_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_tt = TUR_turkish_population_factor_variable }

		set_variable = { TUR_sunni_population_tt = TUR_sunni_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_tt = TUR_orthodox_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_tt = TUR_apostolic_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_judaic_population_tt = TUR_judaic_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_tt = TUR_syriac_population_factor_variable }
		set_variable = { TUR_shia_population_tt = TUR_shia_population_factor }
		set_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_tt = TUR_catholic_population_factor_variable }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_tt = 3 }

			multiply_variable = { TUR_sunni_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_judaic_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_syriac_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_shia_population_tt = 3 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_tt = 3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { original_tag = ALB } }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_armenian_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_jewish_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_arab_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_albanian_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_kurdish_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_assyrian_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_georgian_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_turkish_population_tt = 5 }

			multiply_variable = { TUR_sunni_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_orthodox_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_apostolic_population_tt = 5 }

			multiply_variable = { TUR_shia_population_tt = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { TUR_catholic_population_tt = 5 }
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_political_power_factor = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_adem_i_merkeziyetcilik }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_political_power_factor = TUR_sublime_realm_decentralist_political_power_factor_tt }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_autonomy_in_non_muslim_vilayets }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sublime_realm_political_power_factor = TUR_sublime_realm_decentralist_christian_political_power_factor_tt }
		}
	}
}

TUR_vilayet_centralization_garrison_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = { has_variable = TUR_vc_effect }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_local_manpower = -0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_local_manpower_base = TUR_vc_effect }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_local_manpower_base = 200 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_vc_local_manpower = TUR_vc_local_manpower_base }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = -0.5 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_base = TUR_vc_effect  }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_base = 200 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_vc_state_production_speed_buildings_factor = TUR_vc_state_production_speed_buildings_factor_base }

			#set_variable = { TUR_vc_effect_modifiers = TUR_vc_effect }
			#divide_variable = { TUR_vc_effect_modifiers = 100 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_compliance_gain = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_local_factories = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_local_resources = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_repair_speed_infrastructure_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_repair_speed_arms_factory_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_repair_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0 }
			set_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_decay = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = { occupation_law = autonomous_occupation }
				set_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = -100 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor_temp = -0.6 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				subtract_from_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = 100 }

				set_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = 40 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target_factor_temp = 0.3 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target_factor_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				subtract_from_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = TUR_vc_resistance_target_factor_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = 100 }

				set_variable = { TUR_vc_compliance_gain = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_compliance_gain_factor_temp = 0.02 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_compliance_gain_factor_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				add_to_variable = { TUR_vc_compliance_gain = TUR_vc_compliance_gain_factor_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_compliance_gain = -100 }

				set_variable = { resistance_damage_to_garrison = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison_temp = -0.25 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				subtract_from_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison = TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { occupation_law = foreign_civilian_oversight }
				set_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = -100 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor_temp = -0.75 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				subtract_from_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = 100 }

				set_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = 40 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target_factor_temp = 0.4 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target_factor_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				subtract_from_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = TUR_vc_resistance_target_factor_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_target = 100 }
				
				set_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison_temp = -0.25 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison_temp = TUR_vc_effect }
				subtract_from_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison = TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison_temp }
				divide_variable = { TUR_vc_resistance_damage_to_garrison = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { occupation_law = local_police_force_garrison }
				set_variable = { TUR_vc_required_garrison_factor = -100 }

				check_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level > 0 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_ct_georgian_state_level = TUR_georgian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_ct_georgian_state_level = TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_ct_georgian_state_level = -100000 }
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.TUR_ct_consumer_goods_factor = TUR_ct_georgian_state_level }
		}
		multiply_variable = { TUR_ct_consumer_goods_factor = 2 }
	}
}

TUR_state_proportional_to_religion = {
	every_state = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level > 0 } }
		set_variable = { TUR_apostolic_state_level = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level_net = TUR_armenian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level_net = TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_apostolic_state_level = TUR_armenian_apostolic_state_level_net }
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level > 0 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_greek_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_arab_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = TUR_arab_orthodox_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_south_slavic_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = TUR_south_slavic_orthodox_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_albanian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = TUR_albanian_orthodox_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_georgian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level_net = TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_orthodox_state_level = TUR_georgian_orthodox_state_level_net }
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level > 0 } }
		set_variable = { TUR_judaic_state_level = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level_net = TUR_jewish_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level_net = TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_judaic_state_level = TUR_jewish_judaic_state_level_net }
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level > 0 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_greek_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_greek_sunni_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_sunni_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = TUR_greek_sunni_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_arab_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_arab_sunni_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_sunni_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = TUR_arab_sunni_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_south_slavic_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = TUR_south_slavic_sunni_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_albanian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = TUR_albanian_sunni_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_kurdish_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_kurdish_sunni_state_level_net = 100 }

			set_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_georgian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level }

			add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = TUR_georgian_sunni_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_turkish_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level_net = TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_sunni_state_level = TUR_turkish_sunni_state_level_net }
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level > 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level > 0 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { TUR_catholic_state_level = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level_net = TUR_arab_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level_net = TUR_arab_catholic_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_arab_catholic_state_level_net = 100 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_catholic_state_level = TUR_arab_catholic_state_level_net }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level > 0 } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level_net = TUR_south_slavic_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level_net = TUR_south_slavic_catholic_state_level }

			set_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level_net = TUR_albanian_state_level }
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level_net = TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level }

			add_to_variable = { TUR_catholic_state_level = TUR_albanian_catholic_state_level_net }

				check_variable = { TUR_turkish_shia_state_level > 0 }
			}

			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_turkish_shia_state_level_net = TUR_turkish_shia_state_level }

			add_to_variable = { TUR_shia_state_level = TUR_turkish_shia_state_level_net }
		}
	}
}

		clr_country_flag = TUR_trablusgarp_centralization_select
		random_list = {
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
					    NOT = { any_controlled_state = { has_state_flag = TUR_konstantiniyye } }

					}
				}
				set_country_flag = TUR_edirne_centralization_select
			}
